 paes-myneni made a great start to the match by winning the first set
 unhone pehla set aasaani se 6-4 se apane naam kar liya
 But nadal-lopez struggled fiercely in the second set and won 1–7 in the tiebreaker to tie it 1–1
 haalanki bhartiya jodi teesraa set jald hi 4-6 se haar gai or spanish jodi ko 2-1 kii badhat mil gai
 Again in the fourth set, the Indian pair struggled hard and took a 3–0 lead at one time, but from here Nadal took command and gave the Indian pair five games to win the only game
 bhartiya jodi yah muqabla 6-4, 7-6, 4-6, 4-6 se haari
